add_namespace = korea

country_event = { #간략한 설정
	id = korea.1
	title = korea.1.title
	desc = korea.1.desc
	picture = GFX_event_korea_777
	
	fire_only_once = yes	
    is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					KOR = {
						is_ai = yes
					}
				}
				KOR = {
					add_ideas = KOR_they_will_more_division
				}	
			}
		}
		set_global_flag = TLE_GLOBAL_KOREA_1
	}
	option = { #그래 시작해보자고
		name = korea.1.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_korean_tag = yes
			}
			country_event = {
				id = korea.777
			}
			set_major = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_japan_clique = yes
			}
			country_event = {
				id = TLE_japan.1
			}
			set_major = no
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_chinese_clique = yes
			}
			country_event = {
				id = korea.785
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					is_korean_tag = yes
					is_chinese_clique = yes
					is_japan_clique = yes
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = korea.777
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #그래 시작해보자고
		name = korea.1.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_korean_tag = yes
			}
			set_major = yes
		}
	}
}

	id = korea.106 #동의
	title = korea.106.title
	desc = korea.106.desc
	picture = GFX_TLE_korea_event_none
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #승리다!
		name = korea.106.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				KOR = {
					has_country_flag = FLAG_EVENT_251_A
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = FLAG_EVENT_251_B
					}
				}	
			}
			819 = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = no
			}
			1006 = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				KOR = {
					has_country_flag = FLAG_EVENT_251_B
				}	
			}
			SOV = {
				add_state_core = 561
				add_state_core = 657
				add_state_core = 560
				add_state_core = 409
				add_state_core = 408
				add_state_core = 655
				add_state_core = 537	
				add_state_core = 555	
			}
		}
	}
}

		}
	}
}

country_event = { 
	id = korea.134 #
	title = korea.134.title
	desc = korea.134.desc
	picture = GFX_event_korea_133
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = { #아.
		name = korea.134.a
		set_country_flag = TLE_KANGMYONG_IS_DEAD
		load_focus_tree = kor_kang_dead_focus
		swap_ideas = {
			add_idea = KOR_the_korean_crisis
			remove_idea = KOR_divided_politics
		}
		remove_ideas = KOR_interservice_rivalry_balanced
		remove_ideas = KOR_interservice_rivalry_army_dominant
		remove_ideas = KOR_interservice_rivalry_army_strengthened
		remove_ideas = KOR_interservice_rivalry_navy_strengthened
		remove_ideas = KOR_interservice_rivalry_navy_dominant
		country_lock_all_division_template = yes
		dismantle_faction = yes
	}
}

country_event = { 
	id = korea.244 #서려혁전 준비
	title = korea.244.title
	desc = korea.244.desc
	picture = GFX_TLE_korea_event_none
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #끝까지 간다!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 99
		}
		name = korea.244.a
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_war_support = -0.1
	}
	option = { #
		name = korea.244.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = SOV
			}
			white_peace = SOV
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				SOV = {
					has_cosmetic_tag = SOV_TNO
				}
			}
			annex_country = {
				target = NV1
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
			annex_country = {
				target = KAZ
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				SOV = {
					NOT = {
						has_cosmetic_tag = SOV_TNO
					}
				}
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				target = NV1
				type = annex_everything
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				target = KAZ
				type = annex_everything
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				target = YN1
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		create_wargoal = {
			target = TMS
			type = annex_everything
		}
		create_wargoal = {
			target = BY1
			type = annex_everything
		}
		create_wargoal = {
			target = RUS
			type = annex_everything
		}
		create_wargoal = {
			target = FIN
			type = annex_everything
		}
		SOV = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = SOV
			remove_ideas = TLE_afterwar_idea
			set_capital = { state = 219 }
		}
	}
}

				}
			}

						}

				}

					target = RUS
					transfer_troops = no
				}
			}
		}
		SOV = {
			transfer_state = 214

		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_owned_by = ZZ2
			}

			add_core_of = ZZ2
		} 
	}

		name = korea.300.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = EVENT_KOREA_300_TOOLTIP
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas = KOR_Weakening_the_kingship
			complete_national_focus = KOR_use_the_anti-armed
			news_event = { id = eok_news.49 days = 1 }
			remove_country_leader_role = {
				character = KOR_kim_hui_sun
				ideology = korean_democracy
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = democratic
				last_election = "1932.4.23"
				election_frequency = 48
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			add_country_leader_role = {
				Character = KOR_emperor_yi_jin
				country_leader = {
					#expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = despotism
					desc="YI_CHIN_DESC"
					traits = {
						korea_emperor
					}
				}
				promote_leader = yes
			}	
			add_country_leader_role = {
				Character = KOR_emperor_yi_jin
				country_leader = {
					#expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = korean_democracy
					desc="YI_CHIN_DESC"
					traits = {
						korea_emperor
					}
				}
				promote_leader = yes
			}	
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = democratic
				long_name = "KOR_emperor_ruling_party"
				name = "KOR_emperor_ruling_party"
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = neutrality
				long_name = "KOR_hwangguk_party_long"
				name = "KOR_hwangguk_party"
			}
		}
	}

country_event = { #작계 끝
	id = korea.351
	title = korea.351.title
	desc = korea.351.desc
	picture = GFX_TLE_korea_event_none
	
    is_triggered_only = yes
	
	fire_only_once = no
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			611 = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = no
			}
			612 = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = no
			}
			621 = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = no
			}
			KOR = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = MEN
					autonomous_state = korean_confederation
				}
			}
			MEN = {
				transfer_state = 611
				transfer_state = 612
				transfer_state = 621
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = fascism
					last_election = "1936.1.1"
					election_frequency = 48
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				set_popularities = {
					fascism = 60
					neutrality = 40
				}
			}	
		}	
	}
	
	option = { #그래 시작해보자고
		name = korea.351.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		KOR = {
			declare_war_on = {
				target = MON
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		MEN = {
			declare_war_on = {
				target = MON
				type = annex_everything
			}
			load_oob = "KOR_MEN"
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			MEN = {
				transfer_state = 611
				transfer_state = 612
				transfer_state = 621
			}	
			KOR = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = MEN
					autonomous_state = korean_confederation
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #독궈제국
	id = korea.10007
	title = korea.10007.title
	desc = korea.10007.desc
	picture = GFX_event_korea_777
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = { #
		name = korea.10007.a
		GER = {
			TLE_german_empire_win = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = korea.10007.b
		GER = {
			TLE_german_empire_lose = yes
		}	
	}
	option = { #항복
		name = korea.10007.c
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_in_faction_with = GER
							tag = GER
						}
					}
					white_peace = POL
				}
				GER = {
					transfer_state = 85
					transfer_state = 807
					transfer_state = 86
					transfer_state = 762
					puppet = POL
				}
				POL = {
					set_cosmetic_tag = POL_KINGDOM
					promote_character = POL_karl_albrecht
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						HUN = {
							is_in_faction_with = GER
							has_cosmetic_tag = HUN_EMPIRE
						}
					}
					HUN = {
						transfer_state = 978
						transfer_state = 88
						transfer_state = 91
						transfer_state = 89
						add_state_core = 978
						add_state_core = 88
						add_state_core = 91
						add_state_core = 89
					}
				}
	}	
	option = {
		name = korea.10007.d
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_in_faction_with = GER
							tag = GER
						}
					}
					white_peace = LIT
				}
				GER = {
					transfer_state = 188
					puppet = LIT
				}
				LIT = {
					set_cosmetic_tag = LIT_KINGDOM
					add_ideas = { LIT_karl_gero_idea }
				}
	}	
	option = {
		name = korea.10007.e
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_in_faction_with = GER
							tag = GER
						}
					}
					white_peace = CZE
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						any_country = {
							has_cosmetic_tag = HUN_EMPIRE
						}
					}
					every_country = {
						limit = {
							has_cosmetic_tag = HUN_EMPIRE
						}
						annex_country = {
							target = CZE
							transfer_troops = no
						}
					}	
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							any_country = {
								has_cosmetic_tag = HUN_EMPIRE
							}
						}
						GER = {
							owns_state = 4
						}
					}
					GER = {
						transfer_state = 69
						transfer_state = 74
						transfer_state = 72
						puppet = CZE
					}
					CZE = {
						set_cosmetic_tag = BOH_KINGDOM
						transfer_state = 9
						transfer_state = 75
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							HUN = {
								is_in_faction_with = GER
							}
						}
						HUN = {
							transfer_state = 70
							transfer_state = 71
							transfer_state = 73
							transfer_state = 664
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								HUN = {
									is_in_faction_with = GER
								}
							}
						}
						GER = {
							puppet = SLO
						}
						SLO = {
							transfer_state = 70
							transfer_state = 71
							transfer_state = 73
							transfer_state = 664
							add_state_core = 70

country_event = { #독궈제국
	id = korea.10011
	title = korea.10011.title
	desc = korea.10011.desc
	picture = GFX_event_korea_777
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = { #
		name = korea.10011.a
		set_global_flag = show_peace_popup_alert
		KOR = {
			save_global_event_target_as = winning_country
		}
		JAP = {
			save_global_event_target_as = losing_country
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:losing_country = {
					any_allied_country = {
						has_war_together_with = event_target:losing_country
					}
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = losing_country_multiple
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:winning_country = {
					any_allied_country = {
						has_war_together_with = event_target:winning_country
					}
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = winning_country_multiple
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = no
			}	
			add_to_variable = { global.peace_popup_dirty = 1 }
		}
		log = "war_won"
		set_global_flag = war_won
	}
	option = { #
		name = korea.10011.b
		set_global_flag = show_peace_popup_alert
		KOR = {
			save_global_event_target_as = winning_country
		}
		USA = {
			save_global_event_target_as = losing_country
		}
		if = {

				event_target:losing_country = {
					any_allied_country = {
						has_war_together_with = event_target:losing_country
					}
				}

				event_target:winning_country = {

				}

				is_ai = no
			}

		}
		log = "war_won"
		set_global_flag = war_won
	}
	option = { #
		name = korea.10011.c
		set_global_flag = show_peace_popup_alert
		MSR = {
			save_global_event_target_as = winning_country
		}

			save_global_event_target_as = losing_country

			}

					any_allied_country = {
						has_war_together_with = event_target:winning_country
					}

						has_war_together_with = event_target:losing_country
					}
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = losing_country_multiple
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:winning_country = {
					any_allied_country = {
						has_war_together_with = event_target:winning_country
					}
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = winning_country_multiple
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = no
			}	
			add_to_variable = { global.peace_popup_dirty = 1 }
		}
		log = "war_won"
		set_global_flag = war_won
	}
	option = { #
		name = korea.10012.b
		set_global_flag = show_peace_popup_alert
		GER = {
			save_global_event_target_as = winning_country
		}
		FRA = {
			save_global_event_target_as = losing_country
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:losing_country = {
					any_allied_country = {
						has_war_together_with = event_target:losing_country
					}
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = losing_country_multiple
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:winning_country = {
					any_allied_country = {
						has_war_together_with = event_target:winning_country
					}
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = winning_country_multiple
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = no
			}	
			add_to_variable = { global.peace_popup_dirty = 1 }
		}
		log = "war_won"
		set_global_flag = war_won
	}
	option = { #
		name = korea.10012.c
		set_global_flag = show_peace_popup_alert
		GER = {
			save_global_event_target_as = winning_country
		}
		BEL = {
			save_global_event_target_as = losing_country
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:losing_country = {
					any_allied_country = {
						has_war_together_with = event_target:losing_country
					}
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = losing_country_multiple
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:winning_country = {
					any_allied_country = {
						has_war_together_with = event_target:winning_country
					}
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = winning_country_multiple
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = no
			}	
			add_to_variable = { global.peace_popup_dirty = 1 }
		}
		log = "war_won"
		set_global_flag = war_won
	}
	option = { #
		name = korea.10012.d
	}
	option = { #
		name = korea.10012.e
	}
}
